   āryāvalokiteśvaranāmāṣṭottaraśatādhyeṣaṇāstotraṃ samāptam //	Arya avalokita ISvara nAmA azwa uttara Sata aDyezaNa astotram samAptam //
   Digital Sanskrit Buddhist Canon, Stotra section, text no. 17:	Digitat Sanskrit BudDiH t Canon, Stotra section, text no. 17:
